# Bhagavad Gita Image Prompts for GPT Image 2

Each prompt is standalone and square 1:1. The prompts are verse-specific: no full battlefield, extra characters, or cosmic imagery unless the verse calls for it.

## Chapter 1 - Arjuna Visada Yoga

### 1.1

Bhagavad Gita 1.1. Verse meaning: Dhritarashtra said: Sanjaya, my sons and the sons of Pandu have gathered at Kurukshetra, the field of dharma, ready for war. What did they do? Scene: Immediate scene only: blind elder King Dhritarashtra in a dim Hastinapura royal chamber asks Sanjaya what happened; Sanjaya listens respectfully with a calm visionary presence. No battlefield, no armies, no Krishna, no Arjuna. Tone: quiet royal tension and concern. Square 1:1 composition, cinematic Mahabharata-era Indian epic style, devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic lighting. Characters: Dhritarashtra is a blind elder king, strong but aged, seated with royal gravity; Sanjaya is a mature seer-narrator, calm, focused, respectful. No modern objects, gore, severed bodies, caricature, text, captions, watermarks, logos, or extra fingers.

### 1.2

Bhagavad Gita 1.2. Verse meaning: Sanjaya said: Seeing the Pandava army arranged for battle, King Duryodhana went to his teacher Drona and spoke these words. Scene: Duryodhana speaks to Drona on the battlefield, pointing toward the arranged Pandava army; focus on these commanders and nearby strong warriors, not a wide panorama. Tone: tense pre-battle realism. Square 1:1 composition, cinematic Mahabharata-era Indian epic style, devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic lighting. Characters: Duryodhana is a powerful mature Kaurava prince in armor, proud and tense; Drona is an elderly guru-warrior, stern, strong, white-bearded, armored. Any warriors shown must look strong, disciplined, and battle-ready. No modern objects, gore, severed bodies, caricature, text, captions, watermarks, logos, or extra fingers.

## Chapter 5 - Karma Sanyasa Yoga

### 5.1

Bhagavad Gita 5.1. Verse meaning: Arjuna said: Renunciation of karmas, O Krishna, You praise, and again yoga. Tell me conclusively that which is the better of the two. ## Chapter 14 - Gunatraya Vibhaga Yoga

### 14.1

Bhagavad Gita 14.1. Verse meaning: Sri Krishna said: I will again declare (to you) that supreme knowledge, the best of all knowledge, having known which all the sages have gone to the supreme perfection after this life. Scene: Krishna speaks directly to Arjuna on the chariot; keep the scene focused on their conversation and this verse’s teaching. Tone: wise, heroic, contemplative. Square 1:1 composition, cinematic Mahabharata-era Indian epic style, devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic lighting. Characters: Krishna is the strongest and visually largest presence, mature divine adult, blue skin, broad powerful build, calm face, golden aura, peacock-feather crown, yellow silk; Arjuna is a mature powerful archer with Gandiva, noble face, athletic build, not a teenager. ### 14.2

Bhagavad Gita 14.2. Verse meaning: They who, having taken refuge in this knowledge, have attained to unity with Me, are neither born at the time of creation nor are they disturbed at the time of dissolution. Square 1:1 composition, cinematic Mahabharata-era Indian epic style, devotional realism, rich natural color, dramatic lighting. ### 14.3

## Chapter 15 - Purushottama Yoga

### 15.1
